# SenSALDO, a Swedish sentiment lexicon derived from SALDO
# Base dataset
#
# by Jacobo Rouces, Lars Borin, Nina Tahmasebi and Stian Rødven Eide
#
# version 0.2
# 2019-04-04
# 
# License: CC-BY 4.0 International <https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/>
# 
# If you use this dataset or derivatives of it in publications, 
# please cite one or both of the following publications:
#
# Jacobo Rouces, Nina Tahmasebi, Lars Borin, Stian Rødven Eide 2018. SenSALDO: Creating a sentiment lexicon for Swedish.
# Proceedings of LREC 2018. Miyazaki: ELRA.
#
# @inProceedings{rouces-etal-2018,
#	title		= "{SenSALDO}: Creating a Sentiment Lexicon for {S}wedish",
#	booktitle	= "Proceedings of {LREC} 2018",
#	author		= "Rouces, Jacobo and Tahmasebi, Nina and Borin, Lars and Eide, Stian Rødven",
#	year		= "2018",
#	address		= "Miyazaki",
#       publisher       = "ELRA"
#}
#
# Jacobo Rouces, Lars Borin, Nina Tahmasebi, Stian Rødven Eide 2018. Defining a gold standard for a Swedish sentiment lexicon:
# Towards higher-yield text mining in the digital humanities. Proceedings of DHN 2018. Aachen: CEUR-WS.org.
#
# @inProceedings{rouces-etal-2018,
#	title		= "Defining a Gold Standard for a {S}wedish Sentiment Lexicon: Towards Higher-Yield Text Mining in the Digital Humanities",
#	booktitle	= "Proceedings of {DHN} 2018",
#	author		= "Rouces, Jacobo and Borin, Lars and Tahmasebi, Nina and Eide, Stian Rødven",
#	year		= "2018",
#	address		= "Aachen",
#       publisher       = "CEUR-WS.org"
#}
#
# This is the base dataset from which all other varieties of SenSALDO are derived.
# It assigns prior polarity values to SALDO word senses (not lemmas or text words).
# 
# The labels were first assigned using an automatic method described in the
# first publication above. Subsequently, all positive and negative items and the
# top 2,500 neutral items were manually checked and corrected by Lars Borin,
# resulting in version 0.1 od SenSALDO. This version contains the "transitive
# closure" of SenSALDO v. 0.1 wrt SALDO 2.3. This means that for any text word form
# derivable from any word sense in this version, all its possible word sense assignments
# according to SALDO 2.3 are also present in the dataset.
# This dataset shows only the corrected labels.
#
# Data format:
# <SALDO sense ID>tab<polarity label>
# <polarity label> = "-1" (negative) | "0" (neutral) | "1" (positive)
#
#
